class User {
  @mem static count(next) { return next ?? 0 }
  static refresh() { this.count( this.count() + 1 ) }
  static caller = undefined
  @mem static dto() {
    try {
      const v = myFetchJson('/user/1?q=' + this.count() )
      this.caller.value = false;
      return v;
    catch(e) {
      if (e instanceof Promise && this.caller && $prev) {
        this.caller.value=true
        return $prev
      }
      throw e 
    }
  }

  static name() { return this.dto().name }
}

function UserCard() {
  const isLoadingRef = useRef(false)
  User.caller = isLoadingRef;
  return <div className={isLoadingRef.value ? 'loading' : ''} >
     Name: {User.name()}
    <button onClick={() => { User.refresh() }}>Refresh</button>
  </div>
}
